DE LTAR BYIN GYIS RLOB PAR MDZAD, ,RIG DANG MA RIG YANG DAG LDAN,
,SROG LA SOGS TE BCU GNYIS BSHAD, ,DUS KYI NYIS 'GYUR LAM LA
SOGS, ,DE NYID ZLA BA LA SOGS 'GYUR, ,ZLA BA

LA SOGS GRANGS MNYAM PAS, ,NYI MA BCU GNYIS MING CAN YIN, ,KHYAB
'JUG DE NYID DBYE BA YIS, ,LAM RTZOM PA NI BRTAGS PA YIS, ,DE
NYID DU NI SGRUB PA MCHOG ,SDOM PA YUL ZHES

BSHAD PA YIN, ,SNGAGS DANG DNGOS MED DE BYED PA, ,MGAL ME'I 'KHOR
LO BSKOR DANG MTSUNGS, ,RTOG PA LAS BYUNG DE 'DI NI, ,DNGOS MED
PA NI SGOM PAS SO, ,MA 'ONGS PA YI SKYE BO NI, ,LHA

YI GZUGS LA 'DUD PAR BYED, ,MIG DANG DE BZHIN RNA BA DANG, ,LCE
DANG DE BZHIN LUS DAG DANG, ,PAGS PA RKANG PAR YANG DAG LDAN,
,'DZIN PA DAG NI MI NUS PA, ,LTA DANG NYAN DANG DRI DANG


@180A *, ,RO; ;REG BYA RNAMS NI DNGOS MED PA, ,RANG BZHIN SEMS
MED GYUR BA YI, ,'JIM GZUGS SANGS RGYAS SKU CAN TE, ,'ON KYANG
'GRO BA'I BLA MA'I SKU, ,SANGS RGYAS

BYIN GYIS BYIN RLABS GYIS, ,DE BZHIN SNGAGS SBYOR BDAG NYID CAN,
,DNGOS MED RDO RJE'I SKU NYID YIN, ,SHING DANG SA DANG RIN CHEN
SOGS, ,RANG GI LHA YI GZUGS BYAS LA, ,RANG GI

CHOS NI SPANGS NAS SU, ,TSIG GI LAM DE STON PAR BYED, ,SKU GSUNG
THUGS DANG LDAN PA MCHOG ,CHO 'PHRUL DE 'DRA GA LAS BYUNG, ,DE
NAS DAD SOGS YANG DAG PAS, ,SLAR YANG DE LA

GSOL 'DEBS KYANG, ,GSOL BA 'DEBS PA TZAM GYIS NI, ,DE DANG 'DRA
BAR GA LA 'GYUR, ,PHYI ROL CHOS LA GANG ZHIG DGA', ,LHA RNAMS
THAMS CAD SPONG BA YIN, ,DE LTAR SKU LAS

SKU BYUNG BA, ,DPAL LDAN CHOS 'DI'ANG GSUM GYI LAM, ,BYIN RLABS
PA DAG LONGS SPYOD NA, ,GSUNG GI RDO RJE CAN DU BYED, ,'DAS DANG
MA 'ONGS SANGS RGYAS RNAMS, ,PHYOGS BCU NA NI

GANG BZHUGS PA, ,BYUNG DANG 'BYUNG 'GYUR DE RNAMS NI, ,MI PHYED
GSUM GYI LAM DU 'GYUR, ,YID RTON BDE BA ZHI BDAG NYID, ,DE BZHIN
NYID SHES LAS BYUNG BA, ,YI GE GCIG NI

GSUM DRUG 'DI, ,RANG NYID 'GRO BA'I KHAR BRJOD DO, ,DE YI BYIN
GYIS BRLAB PA'I GNAS, ,RDO RJE MI PHYED RDO RJE CAN, ,GANG GZHAN
SANGS RGYAS KYIS GSUNGS DANG, ,'GRO BA'I SGRAR NI


@180B 'DI GYUR TE, ,DUS GSUM BZHUGS PA'I SANGS RGYAS RNAMS, ,RDO
RJE MI PHYED GSUM RNAL 'BYOR, ,GSUNG GI RDO RJE MI PHYED PA, ,RDO
RJE CAN MCHOG DE BYIN RLOB, ,'JUG PA GNAS PA'I SBYOR BA

DANG, ,LDANG BA DANG NI YANG DAG LDAN, ,GSUNG GI RDO RJE DNGOS
MED PA, ,DE NI SANGS RGYAS BYIN GYIS RLOB, ,JI LTAR 'KHOR LOS
BSGYUR RGYAL NI, ,TSIG GI LAM GYIS LAS BYED 'JUG ,GSUNG

BYIN RLABS PAS SNGAGS PA NI, ,DE BZHIN DON YOD NYID DU BYED, ,DER
NI YANG DAG BSHAD PA 'DI, ,SGRUB PA CHEN PO ZHES BYA BA'O, ,SANGS
RGYAS DE RNAMS BYIN RLOB PA, ,SDOM PA YUL NI

DAM PA'O, ,RDO RJE THUGS NI 'DZIN RGYAL PO, ,DE NI BDAG LA BYIN
RLOB MDZAD, ,MI PHYED RDO RJE GSUM SBYOR BAS, ,NAM MKHA'I KHAMS
DANG MNYAM PA'I GNAS, ,GANG ZHIG BYUNG DANG 'BYUNG

'GYUR BA'I, ,PHYOGS BCUR BZHUGS PA'I SANGS RGYAS RNAMS, ,DE YI
BYIN GYIS BRLAB PA'I GNAS, ,LAN GSUM LAS NI BYUNG BA MDZAD, ,SKU
YIS STON PA'I MDZAD PA MCHOG ,RANG SANGS

RGYAS NI SGOM PA YIN, ,MDO SDE BA DANG NYAN THOS KYI'ANG, ,SMRA
BA SGRUB PA POR GYUR YIN, ,SEMS NI RNAL 'BYOR LDAN MCHOG GIS,
,'GRO BA'I DON NI RAB SGRUB PA'O, ,'GRO 'ONG GNAS DANG

MTSON PA YIS, ,'ON KYANG DE NI GSUNG DU 'GYUR, ,SEMS DANG LUS

RUNG, ,SKU GSUNG THUGS KYI SANGS RGYAS

SOGS; ;RDO RJE GSUM PO MI PHYED BRTAG ,DE 'DAS RMONGS PA'I BDAG
NYID CAN, ,SO SOR RTOG PA 'GAG PAR 'GYUR, ,SKU LA SOGS PA'I
GRANGS MNYAM PAR, ,SANGS RGYAS KYANG NI GANG

RTOG GYUR, ,STONG PA NYID DU SBYOR BA YANG, ,DE NI GSAL BAR THE

PAR MNGON SUM BYED, ,'DAS PA DAG NI DE THAMS

CAD; ;RMONGS PA'I BDAG NYID DE 'GAG 'GYUR, ,NYAN THOS RANG SANGS
RGYAS RNAMS KYI, ,BYANG CHUB BSDUS NAS BSHAD PA YIS, ,'JIG RTEN
PA YI GANG BSHAD PA, ,MDOR BSDUS PA NI

'DI YIN NO, ,SANGS RGYAS YANG NA RDO RJE CHOS, ,YANG NA RDO RJE
SEMS DPA'ANG RUNG, ,RMONGS PAS 'DI LAS 'DAS NA NI, ,DE NI 'GAG
PAR THE TSOM MED, ,DGONGS PA LUNG BSTAN LA GNAS

NAS; ;GSANG BA DAM PA YANG DAG SRUNG, ,LHUN GYIS GRUB PA'I SBYOR
BA YIS, ,DNGOS GRUB MCHOG NI BSGRUB PAR BYA, ,SKU LA SOGS PA'I
GSANG BA MCHOG ,RDO RJE SBYOR BA ZHES BYA BA'I,,

DAM TSIG SGRUB PA'I MCHOG BSTAN PA'I, ,LE'U BCU GNYIS GSUNGS PA
YIN, ,DGONGS PA LUNG BSTAN PA ZHES BYA BA'I RGYUD RDZOGS SO,,
